 Magadha was one of the 16 Mahajanapadas of ancient India
 aadhunik patna or gaya jile isamen shaamil the
 Currently, there is a division in Bihar by this name - Magadha Mandal
 magadh kaa sarvapratham ullekh atharv veda main miltaa he
 Magadha was one of the powerful kingdoms in Buddhist times
 yah dakshini bihar main sthit tha jo baad main uttar bharat kaa sarvaadhik shaktishaalee mahajanapad ban gaya
 The range of Magadha Mahajanapada extended from the Ganges in the north to the Vindhya Mountains in the south, from Champa in the east to the Son River in the west
 magal rajya se jude mahatvapurn tathy:(1)magadh ke sabase pracheen vansh ke sansthaapak brihadrath the
 (2) The capital of Magadha was Giribraj (rajgriha)
 (3)magadh kii gaddi par bimbisar 545 i
 e main baitha tha
 (4) Bimbisara was the founder of the Harayak dynasty
 (5)bimbisar ne brahmadatt ko haraakar ang rajya magadh main mila liya
 (6) Bimbisara was a follower of Buddhism
 (7)bimbisar ne rajgrih kaa nirmaan kar use apni rajdhani banaaya
 (8) Bimbisara ruled Magadha for nearly 52 years
 (9)mahatma buddha kii seva main bimbisar ne rajvaidya jeevak ko bheja
 Even when King Pradyot of Avanti was suffering from Pandya disease, Bimbisara sent Jeevak to serve him
 (10)bimbisar ne vaivaahik sambandh sthapit kar apane samrajya kaa vistaar kiya
 He married Mahakoshla, sister of Kosala Naresh Prasenjit, Chellana, daughter of Chetak of Vaishali and Princess Kshema of Madra Desh (modern Punjab)
 (11)bimbisar kii hatya uske putr ajatshatru ne kar di or vah 493 i
 e main magadh kii gaddi par baitha
 (12) Ajatashatru's surname was Kunik
 (13)ajatshatru ne 32 saalon tak magadh par shashan kiya
 (14) Ajatashatru was a follower of Jainism in the beginning
 (15)ajatshatru ke suyogy mantri kaa naam varshkaar tha

 e main kar di or vah magadh kii gaddi par baitha
 (17) Udayin founded the Pataligram
 (18)udayin bhi jain dharm kaa anuyaayi tha
 (19) The last king of the Hrayaka dynasty was Udayin's son Nagadashak
 (20)nagdashak ko uske amaatya shishunag ne 412 i
 e main apdasth karke magadh par shishunath vansh kii sthapana kii
 (21) Shishunath removed his capital from Pataliputra and established it at Vaishali

 'nasa ke prashaasak charles bolden or isro ke adhyaksh ke radhakrishnan ne ek international samjhaute par bhi hastakshar kiye, jisamen bataaya gaya he ki donon agenciyaan ‘nasa-isro synthetic epperchar radar’ (enaiesr) mishan par kis tarah ek saath kaam karengi
 NISAR is targeted to be launched in the year 2020

 The NASA administrator said, "this partnership will benefit both countries and the whole world
" ’mars varking group kii bhoomika laal grah ke bare main anveshan karne ke sambandh main donon agenciyon ke madhya vaigyanik, kaarykram sambandhi or praudyogiki aadhaarit saajha lakshyon kii pahchaan or unka karyanvayan karne kii disha main hogi

 tippaniyan Under the NPS scheme, investments have to be contributed till the age of sixty years
 enpies main nivesh kii nunatam raashi chah hajaar rupee he
 Currently, there are three investment fund options
 sarkari pratibhuti fund, nishchit aay ke saadhan or equity fund

 vah bhi sirf index fund ke madhyam se
 At the age of sixty years, a minimum of 40 percent of the amount of maturity is to be kept as annual allowance and the remaining amount is paid in lump sum

 05AM: Sri Sri Ravi Shankar reached Tihar, but returned without meeting Anna Hazare notebandi ke is daur main local storon or sabji kii dukaanon par ap aadhaarit pement yaa plastic karency ke badhate chalan ke bich yahaan ke ek shaks ne apane andaaj main hi iskaa muzahra kiya
 After using a public toilet, this man cut a check for five rupees in the name of "public toilet" as payment
 is sambandh main do disambar ko fasebuk yujar bi muralidharan ne post karke us check ko soshal media par share kiya or uske baad soshal netwarking website par share kiya
 The comments muralidharan ne fasebuk par likhaa, ''desh cashles iconomi kii taraf bad rahaa he
 Therefore, after making a public toilet in Madurai, he gave a check of five rupees
 '' It is worth mentioning that on November 8, PM Narendra Modi announced demonetisation of 500 and 1000 rupees
 uske baad se nae noton ko paane ke liye bainkon or atm kii kataron main lambii line dekhne ko mil rahi hai
 In this regard, on December 2, Facebook user b Muralitharan posted and shared that check on social media and then shared it on the social networking website
 tippaniyan Muralitharan wrote on Facebook, "the country is moving towards a cashless economy
 is lihaaj se madurai main public toilet karne ke baad paanch rupee kaa check diya
 '' ullekhneey he ki aath november ko piem narendra modi ne 500 or 1000 rupee kii notebandi kii ghoshnaa kii
 Since then, long lines have been seen in the queues of banks and atms to get new notes

 The Pune Warriors India team defeated Kings XI Punjab by 22 runs in the fifth edition of the Indian Premier League (IPL) played on Sunday at the newly formed Subrata Roy Sahara Stadium
 is tarah pune ne lagaataar duusari jeet darj kii
 Marlon Samuels was adjudged Man of the Match for his innings of 46 runs and taking one wicket
 toss jitkar pehle ballebaaji karte hue pune warirs ne nirdhaarit 20 overon main chah vaket ke nuksaan par 166 ran banaae
 In response, the team of Kings XI Punjab came out to bat, scoring only 144 runs for the loss of eight wickets in 20 overs
 kings ilevan punjab kii ore se bipul sharma ne 35, mandeep singh ne 24 or abhishek nair ne 24, david hasi ne 18 or piyush chawla ne 16 ranon kaa yogadan diya
 Kings XI had a poor start and their opening two batsmen were runouts
 paul valthti ek ran ke nijee yoga par tisare over main jabaki adam gilcrist chah ran ke nijee yoga par chauthe over main ranout hue
 For Pune Warriors, Rahul Sharma took two wickets while Marlon Samuels, Ashok Dinda, Ashish Nehra and Jesse Ryder had one success each
 isse pehle toss jitkar pehle ballebaaji karte hue pune warirs ne nirdhaarit 20 overon main chah wicket ke nuksaan par 166 ran banaae
 Pune's first wicket fell as Sourav Ganguly
 lay main dikh rahe ganguli 20 ran banaakar damitri mascarenhas kii gend par paul valthti ke haathon lapke gaye
 Ganguly faced 18 balls in his innings, hitting three fours
 rider ne aath ran banaae
 He was run out by Praveen Kumar for a total of 32 runs
 marlan samuels ne 39 gendon main chaar chauke or do chakke kii madad se tabadatod pari khelte hue 46 ran banaae
 He was bowled by Harmeet Singh
 fagryusan 3 ran ke nijee yoga par harmit singh kii gend par unheen ko kaich thama baithe
 Rabin Uthappa scored 40 runs in 33 balls with the help of two fours and two sixes
 uthppa ko harmit singh ne bold kiya
 Steven Smith scored 25 runs in 12 balls with the help of three sixes
 manish pandeya 12 ran banaakar naabad rahe
 The comments kings ilevan kii ore se harmit singh ko teen safalataa mili jabaki damitri mascarenhas or fahonor ko ek wicket mila
 This is the second consecutive win for the Pune Warriors India team, who defeated the Mumbai Indians team, the first contenders in the fifth edition, to be one of the strongest contenders for the title
 vahiin kings ilevan kii yah lagaataar duusari haar he
